<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">East Coast Greenway</h1> <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div> <div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold;background:Silver">East Coast Greenway</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<a class="image" href="/wiki/File:American_Tobacco_Trail.jpg"><img alt="American Tobacco Trail.jpg" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="1728" height="333" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/American_Tobacco_Trail.jpg/250px-American_Tobacco_Trail.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/American_Tobacco_Trail.jpg/375px-American_Tobacco_Trail.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/American_Tobacco_Trail.jpg/500px-American_Tobacco_Trail.jpg 2x" width="250"/></a><div>The <a href="/wiki/American_Tobacco_Trail" title="American Tobacco Trail">American Tobacco Trail</a>, which forms 17.5 miles (28.2 km) of the East Coast Greenway in North Carolina</div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Length</th><td>
3,000 miles (4,800 km)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Trailhead" title="Trailhead">Trailheads</a></th><td>
<a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">Maine</a>/<a href="/wiki/Canada%E2%80%93United_States_border" title="Canada–United States border">Canada–US border</a>-<a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">Florida</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Use</th><td>
Multi-use, non-motorized</td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background:Silver">Elevation</th></tr><tr><th scope="row">Highest point</th><td>
<a href="/wiki/West_Boylston,_Massachusetts" title="West Boylston, Massachusetts">West Boylston, Massachusetts</a>, 680 ft (210 m)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Lowest point</th><td>
Many locations within 10 feet (3.0 m) or less of sea level</td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background:Silver">Hiking details</th></tr><tr><th scope="row">Season</th><td>
Variable, depending on latitude</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Hazards_of_outdoor_recreation" title="Hazards of outdoor recreation">Hazards</a></th><td>
Weather, <a href="/wiki/Tick-borne_disease" title="Tick-borne disease">tick-borne diseases</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Poison_ivy" title="Poison ivy">poison ivy</a></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>East Coast Greenway</b> is a 3,000-mile (4,800 km) <a href="/wiki/Bicycle_boulevard" title="Bicycle boulevard">biking and walking route</a> linking the major cities of the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">Atlantic</a> coast of the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, from <a href="/wiki/Calais,_Maine" title="Calais, Maine">Calais, Maine</a>, to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Key_West,_Florida" title="Key West, Florida">Key West, Florida</a>. The spine route and branching complementary routes are for non-motorized human transportation for everything from local commutes to long-distance trips. 
</p><p>The nonprofit East Coast Greenway Alliance was created in 1991. The entire route has been selected. As of July 2017, 900 miles (1,450 km), or 32 percent of the route, is off-road on traffic-protected greenways. The vision is for the entire trail to be off-road.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ECG_E-News_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-ECG_E-News-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ECGW_Cabot_Tour_9_truck_jeh.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2086" data-file-width="2483" height="185" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/ECGW_Cabot_Tour_9_truck_jeh.jpg/220px-ECGW_Cabot_Tour_9_truck_jeh.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/ECGW_Cabot_Tour_9_truck_jeh.jpg/330px-ECGW_Cabot_Tour_9_truck_jeh.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/ECGW_Cabot_Tour_9_truck_jeh.jpg/440px-ECGW_Cabot_Tour_9_truck_jeh.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ECGW_Cabot_Tour_9_truck_jeh.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Looking east as a Greenway tour approaches the bridge over the <a href="/wiki/Hackensack_River" title="Hackensack River">Hackensack River</a> in New Jersey</div></div></div>
<p>In 1991, a group of cyclists and <a href="/wiki/Long-distance_trail" title="Long-distance trail">long-distance trail</a> enthusiasts met in <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a> and formed a national non-profit organization, the East Coast Greenway Alliance (ECGA), to plan and promote a greenway linking existing and planned trails into a contiguous "spine route" between Atlantic coast cities.
</p><p>In summer 1992, the ECGA sent nine cyclists from <a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">Boston</a>, New York City, <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">Vermont</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a>, on a 30-day "exploratory" <a href="/wiki/Bicycle_touring" title="Bicycle touring">cycle tour</a>.
</p><p>In 1993, tours went along the route to explore options and promote the idea of the greenway. In 1994, the first promotional tour took place from <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">Maine</a> to Washington, D.C. "East Coast Greenway" became a trademark in 1995.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>
</p><p>The first five trail segments were designated in 1996. These segments were the <a href="/wiki/Baltimore_%26_Annapolis_Trail" title="Baltimore &amp; Annapolis Trail">Baltimore &amp; Annapolis Trail</a> in <a href="/wiki/Maryland" title="Maryland">Maryland</a>, the Charter Oak Greenway in <a href="/wiki/Connecticut" title="Connecticut">Connecticut</a>, the Coventry Greenway in <a href="/wiki/Rhode_Island" title="Rhode Island">Rhode Island</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Farmington_Canal_Heritage_Trail" title="Farmington Canal Heritage Trail">Farmington Canal Greenway</a> in Connecticut, and the <a href="/wiki/D%26R_Canal_Trail" title="D&amp;R Canal Trail">Delaware &amp; Raritan Canal Trail</a> in <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">New Jersey</a>. These trails make up 56 miles (90 km) of the greenway.
</p><p>Between 1997 and 2000, about 150 miles (240 km) of trail segments were designated throughout the region. In 2000, Amtrak became a partner, helping to open access to various parts of the route. Between February and June 2000, the ECG Wave non-motorized relay carried a bottle of seawater from Key West to <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a> along the route of the ECG. From 2001 to 2004, another 173 miles (278 km) were designated, and multiple states stepped in to help finalize their section of the route. This brought in more partnerships with government organizations, such as <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Department_of_Transportation" title="New Jersey Department of Transportation">NJDOT</a>, that would be essential for trail development. In 2003, members of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">House of Representatives</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">Senate</a> signed letters to <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">President Bush</a> in support of the greenway.
</p><p>In 2004, seven cyclists rode the entire route, from Key West to Calais, in 55 days. Later that year, the first Maine-to-Florida tour was held; four cyclists completed the event in 52 days, raising $75,000. In the following years, more people would complete the ride outside of ECG events. A 2005 <a href="/wiki/GQ" title="GQ"><i>GQ</i> magazine</a> article about a ride by <a href="/wiki/Wil_S._Hylton" title="Wil S. Hylton">Wil Hylton</a> brought national attention to the greenway.
</p><p>The entire spine route was finalized and mapped in 2008. The accessibility of the trail expanded with support of the states, and more events were held each year.
</p><p>As of 2017, 32 percent of the greenway is off-road.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> Efforts to increase the amount of off-road routes are continuing.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Route">Route</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Route">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Major cities connected by the "spine route" are:
</p>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;">
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/Calais,_Maine" title="Calais, Maine">Calais, Maine</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bangor,_Maine" title="Bangor, Maine">Bangor, Maine</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Augusta,_Maine" title="Augusta, Maine">Augusta, Maine</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Portland,_Maine" title="Portland, Maine">Portland, Maine</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Portsmouth,_New_Hampshire" title="Portsmouth, New Hampshire">Portsmouth, New Hampshire</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Newburyport,_Massachusetts" title="Newburyport, Massachusetts">Newburyport, Massachusetts</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Boston,_Massachusetts" title="Boston, Massachusetts">Boston, Massachusetts</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Worcester,_Massachusetts" title="Worcester, Massachusetts">Worcester, Massachusetts</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Providence,_Rhode_Island" title="Providence, Rhode Island">Providence, Rhode Island</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hartford,_Connecticut" title="Hartford, Connecticut">Hartford, Connecticut</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/New_Haven,_Connecticut" title="New Haven, Connecticut">New Haven, Connecticut</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Stamford,_Connecticut" title="Stamford, Connecticut">Stamford, Connecticut</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York, New York</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jersey_City,_New_Jersey" title="Jersey City, New Jersey">Jersey City, New Jersey</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Newark,_New_Jersey" title="Newark, New Jersey">Newark, New Jersey</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/New_Brunswick,_New_Jersey" title="New Brunswick, New Jersey">New Brunswick, New Jersey</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Trenton,_New_Jersey" title="Trenton, New Jersey">Trenton, New Jersey</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Philadelphia,_Pennsylvania" title="Philadelphia, Pennsylvania">Philadelphia, Pennsylvania</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_Delaware" title="Wilmington, Delaware">Wilmington, Delaware</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Baltimore,_Maryland" title="Baltimore, Maryland">Baltimore, Maryland</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Annapolis,_Maryland" title="Annapolis, Maryland">Annapolis, Maryland</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Richmond,_Virginia" title="Richmond, Virginia">Richmond, Virginia</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Durham,_North_Carolina" title="Durham, North Carolina">Durham, North Carolina</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Raleigh,_North_Carolina" title="Raleigh, North Carolina">Raleigh, North Carolina</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fayetteville,_North_Carolina" title="Fayetteville, North Carolina">Fayetteville, North Carolina</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_North_Carolina" title="Wilmington, North Carolina">Wilmington, North Carolina</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina" title="Myrtle Beach, South Carolina">Myrtle Beach, South Carolina</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Charleston,_South_Carolina" title="Charleston, South Carolina">Charleston, South Carolina</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Savannah,_Georgia" title="Savannah, Georgia">Savannah, Georgia</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brunswick,_Georgia" title="Brunswick, Georgia">Brunswick, Georgia</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jacksonville,_Florida" title="Jacksonville, Florida">Jacksonville, Florida</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/St._Augustine,_Florida" title="St. Augustine, Florida">St. Augustine, Florida</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Daytona_Beach,_Florida" title="Daytona Beach, Florida">Daytona Beach, Florida</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Titusville,_Florida" title="Titusville, Florida">Titusville, Florida</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Melbourne,_Florida" title="Melbourne, Florida">Melbourne, Florida</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fort_Pierce,_Florida" title="Fort Pierce, Florida">Fort Pierce, Florida</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/West_Palm_Beach,_Florida" title="West Palm Beach, Florida">West Palm Beach, Florida</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Boca_Raton,_Florida" title="Boca Raton, Florida">Boca Raton, Florida</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fort_Lauderdale,_Florida" title="Fort Lauderdale, Florida">Fort Lauderdale, Florida</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Miami,_Florida" title="Miami, Florida">Miami, Florida</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Key_West,_Florida" title="Key West, Florida">Key West, Florida</a></li></ol>
</div><p>Other cities may be connected by "alternate route" in some locations. More information about the route can be found online at greenway.org; an online mapping tool is available at map.greenway.org.
</p><h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Active_segments">Active segments</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Active segments">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As of 2016, designated trails and locations of the East Coast Greenway include:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="New_England_region">New England region</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: New England region">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Maine">Maine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Maine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:381px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:East_Coast_Greenway_Maine.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2160" data-file-width="3840" height="213" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/East_Coast_Greenway_Maine.jpg/379px-East_Coast_Greenway_Maine.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/East_Coast_Greenway_Maine.jpg/569px-East_Coast_Greenway_Maine.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/East_Coast_Greenway_Maine.jpg/758px-East_Coast_Greenway_Maine.jpg 2x" width="379"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:East_Coast_Greenway_Maine.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ride on the East Coast Greenway in Maine</div></div></div>
<p>Travelers start in <a href="/wiki/Calais,_Maine" title="Calais, Maine">Calais, Maine</a>, at the <a href="/wiki/Canada%E2%80%93United_States_border" title="Canada–United States border">Canada–US border</a>, and pedal southwest through <a href="/wiki/Ellsworth,_Maine" title="Ellsworth, Maine">Ellsworth</a>, where they can stay on the inland spine route through <a href="/wiki/Bangor,_Maine" title="Bangor, Maine">Bangor</a> or veer off along a 150-mile (240 km) coastal route. The routes rejoin north of <a href="/wiki/Portland,_Maine" title="Portland, Maine">Portland</a>, then head on towards <a href="/wiki/Portsmouth,_New_Hampshire" title="Portsmouth, New Hampshire">Portsmouth, New Hampshire</a>. The route through Maine is 350 miles (560 km) long, and 39% of that is currently off-road.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Calais Waterfront Walkway – <a href="/wiki/Calais,_Maine" title="Calais, Maine">Calais</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Moosehorn_National_Wildlife_Refuge" title="Moosehorn National Wildlife Refuge">Moosehorn National Wildlife Refuge Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Baring_Plantation,_Maine" title="Baring Plantation, Maine">Baring</a></li>
<li>Downeast Sunrise Trail – <a href="/wiki/Washington_County,_Maine" title="Washington County, Maine">Washington</a> &amp; <a href="/wiki/Hancock_County,_Maine" title="Hancock County, Maine">Hancock</a> counties</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kennebec_River" title="Kennebec River">Kennebec River</a> Rail Trail – <a href="/wiki/Augusta,_Maine" title="Augusta, Maine">Augusta</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hallowell,_Maine" title="Hallowell, Maine">Hallowell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Farmingdale,_Maine" title="Farmingdale, Maine">Farmingdale</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Gardiner,_Maine" title="Gardiner, Maine">Gardiner</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Rotary_Centennial_Trail&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Rotary Centennial Trail (page does not exist)">Rotary Centennial Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Benton,_Maine" title="Benton, Maine">Benton</a></li>
<li>Lewiston Riverside Trail – <a href="/wiki/Lewiston,_Maine" title="Lewiston, Maine">Lewiston</a></li>
<li>Lisbon Trail – <a href="/wiki/Lisbon,_Maine" title="Lisbon, Maine">Lisbon</a></li>
<li>Topsham Trail – <a href="/wiki/Topsham,_Maine" title="Topsham, Maine">Topsham</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Androscoggin_River" title="Androscoggin River">Androscoggin River</a> Bicycle Path – <a href="/wiki/Brunswick,_Maine" title="Brunswick, Maine">Brunswick</a></li>
<li>Beth Condon Memorial Pathway – <a href="/wiki/Yarmouth,_Maine" title="Yarmouth, Maine">Yarmouth</a></li>
<li>Martin's Point Bridge – <a href="/wiki/Falmouth,_Maine" title="Falmouth, Maine">Falmouth</a> to <a href="/wiki/Portland,_Maine" title="Portland, Maine">Portland</a></li>
<li>Eastern Promenade/Connector/Back Cove Trail – Portland</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=South_Portland_Green_Belt&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="South Portland Green Belt (page does not exist)">South Portland Green Belt</a> – <a href="/wiki/South_Portland,_Maine" title="South Portland, Maine">South Portland</a></li>
<li>Eastern Trail – <a href="/wiki/Scarborough,_Maine" title="Scarborough, Maine">Scarborough</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saco,_Maine" title="Saco, Maine">Saco</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Old_Orchard_Beach,_Maine" title="Old Orchard Beach, Maine">Old Orchard Beach</a></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Hampshire">New Hampshire</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: New Hampshire">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Riders enter the state on the <a href="/wiki/Memorial_Bridge_(Portsmouth,_New_Hampshire)" title="Memorial Bridge (Portsmouth, New Hampshire)">Memorial Bridge</a> in <a href="/wiki/Portsmouth,_New_Hampshire" title="Portsmouth, New Hampshire">Portsmouth, New Hampshire</a>, and follow the coastline to <a href="/wiki/Seabrook,_New_Hampshire" title="Seabrook, New Hampshire">Seabrook</a> and then on to the Massachusetts border. New Hampshire has the shortest portion of the greenway: about 17 miles (27 km), all on-road.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>New Hampshire Seacoast Greenway</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Massachusetts">Massachusetts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Massachusetts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mt_Tom_Rd_ECGW_NR_jeh.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="4000" data-file-width="3000" height="293" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Mt_Tom_Rd_ECGW_NR_jeh.jpg/220px-Mt_Tom_Rd_ECGW_NR_jeh.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Mt_Tom_Rd_ECGW_NR_jeh.jpg/330px-Mt_Tom_Rd_ECGW_NR_jeh.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Mt_Tom_Rd_ECGW_NR_jeh.jpg/440px-Mt_Tom_Rd_ECGW_NR_jeh.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mt_Tom_Rd_ECGW_NR_jeh.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Looking northeast at an ECGW sign</div></div></div>
<p>The greenway enters the state near <a href="/wiki/Salisbury,_Massachusetts" title="Salisbury, Massachusetts">Salisbury, Massachusetts</a>, and heads south towards <a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">Boston</a> and then to <a href="/wiki/Waltham,_Massachusetts" title="Waltham, Massachusetts">Waltham</a>. Next, it travels on from <a href="/wiki/Worcester,_Massachusetts" title="Worcester, Massachusetts">Worcester</a> to the Rhode Island border. The route travels along the Charles River and past the birthplace of the <a href="/wiki/Technological_and_industrial_history_of_the_United_States" title="Technological and industrial history of the United States">American Industrial Revolution</a>. 
</p>
<ul><li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Border_to_Boston_Trail&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Border to Boston Trail (page does not exist)">Border to Boston Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Salisbury,_Massachusetts" title="Salisbury, Massachusetts">Salisbury</a>, <a href="/wiki/Newburyport,_Massachusetts" title="Newburyport, Massachusetts">Newburyport</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wenham,_Massachusetts" title="Wenham, Massachusetts">Wenham</a>, <a href="/wiki/Danvers,_Massachusetts" title="Danvers, Massachusetts">Danvers</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Peabody,_Massachusetts" title="Peabody, Massachusetts">Peabody</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Peabody_Independence_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Peabody Independence Greenway (page does not exist)">Peabody Independence Greenway</a> – Peabody</li>
<li>Salem Bike Path – <a href="/wiki/Salem,_Massachusetts" title="Salem, Massachusetts">Salem</a></li>
<li>Lynn Beach Promenade – <a href="/wiki/Lynn,_Massachusetts" title="Lynn, Massachusetts">Lynn</a></li>
<li>Lynnway Sidepath – Lynn</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Northern_Strand_Community_Trail" title="Northern Strand Community Trail">Northern Strand Community Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Malden,_Massachusetts" title="Malden, Massachusetts">Malden</a> to <a href="/wiki/Everett,_Massachusetts" title="Everett, Massachusetts">Everett</a></li>
<li>Everett Bike Path – Everett</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=North_Bank_Park_Path&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="North Bank Park Path (page does not exist)">North Bank Park Path</a> – <a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">Boston</a> to <a href="/wiki/Cambridge,_Massachusetts" title="Cambridge, Massachusetts">Cambridge</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Charles_River_Bike_Path" title="Charles River Bike Path">Charles River Bike Path</a> – Boston, <a href="/wiki/Watertown,_Massachusetts" title="Watertown, Massachusetts">Watertown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Newton,_Massachusetts" title="Newton, Massachusetts">Newton</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Waltham,_Massachusetts" title="Waltham, Massachusetts">Waltham</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Blackstone_River_Greenway" title="Blackstone River Greenway">Blackstone River Bikeway</a> – <a href="/wiki/Worcester,_Massachusetts" title="Worcester, Massachusetts">Worcester</a> to <a href="/wiki/Millbury,_Massachusetts" title="Millbury, Massachusetts">Millbury</a> &amp; <a href="/wiki/Uxbridge,_Massachusetts" title="Uxbridge, Massachusetts">Uxbridge</a> to <a href="/wiki/Blackstone,_Massachusetts" title="Blackstone, Massachusetts">Blackstone</a></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Rhode_Island">Rhode Island</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Rhode Island">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The greenway enters from Massachusetts on the <a href="/wiki/Blackstone_River_Greenway" title="Blackstone River Greenway">Blackstone River Bikeway</a> and follows the historic <a href="/wiki/Blackstone_Canal" title="Blackstone Canal">Blackstone Canal</a>. It travels down to <a href="/wiki/Pawtucket,_Rhode_Island" title="Pawtucket, Rhode Island">Pawtucket</a> and then into <a href="/wiki/Providence,_Rhode_Island" title="Providence, Rhode Island">Providence</a>, where it goes around <a href="/wiki/India_Point_Park" title="India Point Park">India Point Park</a> at <a href="/wiki/Narragansett_Bay" title="Narragansett Bay">Narragansett Bay</a>, and then on to <a href="/wiki/Cranston,_Rhode_Island" title="Cranston, Rhode Island">Cranston</a>. This 49-mile (79 km) section of greenway is 52% off-road, with another 30% being developed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Blackstone_River_Greenway" title="Blackstone River Greenway">Blackstone River Greenway</a> – <a href="/wiki/Woonsocket,_Rhode_Island" title="Woonsocket, Rhode Island">Woonsocket</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cumberland,_Rhode_Island" title="Cumberland, Rhode Island">Cumberland</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Lincoln,_Rhode_Island" title="Lincoln, Rhode Island">Lincoln</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/East_Bay_Bike_Path" title="East Bay Bike Path">East Bay Bike Path</a> – <a href="/wiki/East_Providence,_Rhode_Island" title="East Providence, Rhode Island">East Providence</a> to <a href="/wiki/Warren,_Rhode_Island" title="Warren, Rhode Island">Warren</a></li>
<li>Providence Riverwalk – <a href="/wiki/Providence,_Rhode_Island" title="Providence, Rhode Island">Providence</a></li>
<li>Cranston Bike Path – <a href="/wiki/Cranston,_Rhode_Island" title="Cranston, Rhode Island">Cranston</a></li>
<li>Warwick Greenway – <a href="/wiki/Warwick,_Rhode_Island" title="Warwick, Rhode Island">Warwick</a></li>
<li>West Warwick Greenway – <a href="/wiki/West_Warwick,_Rhode_Island" title="West Warwick, Rhode Island">West Warwick</a></li>
<li>Coventry Greenway – <a href="/wiki/Coventry,_Rhode_Island" title="Coventry, Rhode Island">Coventry</a></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Connecticut">Connecticut</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Connecticut">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Connecticut has the most rural stretch of trail in the region. It runs through historic mill towns, such as <a href="/wiki/Willimantic,_Connecticut" title="Willimantic, Connecticut">Willimantic</a>, and major cities like <a href="/wiki/Hartford,_Connecticut" title="Hartford, Connecticut">Hartford</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Haven,_Connecticut" title="New Haven, Connecticut">New Haven</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bridgeport,_Connecticut" title="Bridgeport, Connecticut">Bridgeport</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Stamford,_Connecticut" title="Stamford, Connecticut">Stamford</a>. Users can travel on the <a href="/wiki/Farmington_Canal_Heritage_Trail" title="Farmington Canal Heritage Trail">Farmington Canal Greenway</a> to get to New Haven from <a href="/wiki/Simsbury,_Connecticut" title="Simsbury, Connecticut">Simsbury</a> and then ride along the <a href="/wiki/Long_Island_Sound" title="Long Island Sound">Long Island Sound</a> as they exit the state. Currently, 28% of the 198-mile (319 km) route is off-road, with an additional 28% in development.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Moosup_Valley_State_Park_Trail" title="Moosup Valley State Park Trail">Moosup Valley State Park Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Plainfield,_Connecticut" title="Plainfield, Connecticut">Plainfield</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Quinebaug_River" title="Quinebaug River">Quinebaug River Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Killingly,_Connecticut" title="Killingly, Connecticut">Killingly</a></li>
<li>Tracy Road Smart Parks Trail – Killingly to <a href="/wiki/Putnam,_Connecticut" title="Putnam, Connecticut">Putnam</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Air_Line_State_Park_Trail" title="Air Line State Park Trail">Air Line State Park Trail North</a> – <a href="/wiki/Windham_County,_Connecticut" title="Windham County, Connecticut">Windham County</a></li>
<li>Veterans Memorial Greenway – <a href="/wiki/Willimantic,_Connecticut" title="Willimantic, Connecticut">Willimantic</a></li>
<li>Charter Oak Greenway – <a href="/wiki/Manchester,_Connecticut" title="Manchester, Connecticut">Manchester</a> to <a href="/wiki/East_Hartford,_Connecticut" title="East Hartford, Connecticut">East Hartford</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Founders_Bridge" title="Founders Bridge">Founders Bridge Path</a> – <a href="/wiki/Hartford,_Connecticut" title="Hartford, Connecticut">Hartford</a> to East Hartford</li>
<li>Phoenix Plaza – Hartford</li>
<li>Travelers Plaza – Hartford</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bushnell_Park" title="Bushnell Park">Bushnell Park Path</a> – Hartford</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Farmington_Canal_Heritage_Trail" title="Farmington Canal Heritage Trail">Farmington Canal Heritage Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Simsbury,_Connecticut" title="Simsbury, Connecticut">Simsbury</a>, <a href="/wiki/Avon,_Connecticut" title="Avon, Connecticut">Avon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Farmington,_Connecticut" title="Farmington, Connecticut">Farmington</a>, <a href="/wiki/Southington,_Connecticut" title="Southington, Connecticut">Southington</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cheshire,_Connecticut" title="Cheshire, Connecticut">Cheshire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hamden,_Connecticut" title="Hamden, Connecticut">Hamden</a>, to <a href="/wiki/New_Haven,_Connecticut" title="New Haven, Connecticut">New Haven</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Savin_Rock" title="Savin Rock">Savin Rock Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/West_Haven,_Connecticut" title="West Haven, Connecticut">West Haven</a></li>
<li>Long Wharf Nature Preserve Trail – New Haven</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Silver_Sands_State_Park" title="Silver Sands State Park">Silver Sands State Park Path</a> – <a href="/wiki/Milford,_Connecticut" title="Milford, Connecticut">Milford</a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mid-Atlantic_region">Mid-Atlantic region</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Mid-Atlantic region">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="New_York">New York</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: New York">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:New_Rochelle;_ECG_Bike_Sign.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3864" data-file-width="5152" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/New_Rochelle%3B_ECG_Bike_Sign.jpg/220px-New_Rochelle%3B_ECG_Bike_Sign.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/New_Rochelle%3B_ECG_Bike_Sign.jpg/330px-New_Rochelle%3B_ECG_Bike_Sign.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/New_Rochelle%3B_ECG_Bike_Sign.jpg/440px-New_Rochelle%3B_ECG_Bike_Sign.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:New_Rochelle;_ECG_Bike_Sign.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>East Coast Greenway bicycle sign between New Rock City and Trump Plaza in downtown <a href="/wiki/New_Rochelle,_New_York" title="New Rochelle, New York">New Rochelle, New York</a></div></div></div>
<p>The New York segments starts in <a href="/wiki/Westchester_County,_New_York" title="Westchester County, New York">Westchester County</a> and heads south into <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a> through <a href="/wiki/The_Bronx" title="The Bronx">the Bronx</a> and <a href="/wiki/Manhattan" title="Manhattan">Manhattan</a>. The route travels down sections of <a href="/wiki/Broadway_(Manhattan)" title="Broadway (Manhattan)">Broadway</a> and along the <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">Hudson River</a>, which travelers can cross via the <a href="/wiki/George_Washington_Bridge" title="George Washington Bridge">George Washington Bridge</a> or by taking a <a href="/wiki/NY_Waterway" title="NY Waterway">NY Waterway</a> ferry into New Jersey. New York is home to 44 miles (71 km) of greenway, with 62% of the route, the highest percentage on the greenway, being off-road. In Manhattan, 90% of the trail is off-road.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Shore Road Greenway – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bronx" title="Bronx">Bronx</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pelham_Parkway" title="Pelham Parkway">Pelham Parkway</a> Greenway – Bronx</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bronx_Park" title="Bronx Park">Bronx Park</a> Greenway – Bronx</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bronx_River" title="Bronx River">Bronx River</a> Pathway – Bronx</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mosholu_Parkway" title="Mosholu Parkway">Mosholu Parkway</a> Greenway – Bronx</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Van_Cortlandt_Park" title="Van Cortlandt Park">Van Cortlandt Park</a> Greenway – Bronx</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hudson_River_Greenway" title="Hudson River Greenway">Hudson River Greenway</a> – <a href="/wiki/Manhattan" title="Manhattan">Manhattan</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Randall%27s_Island" title="Randall's Island">Randall's Island</a> Greenway – Manhattan</li>
<li>103rd Street Footbridge – Manhattan</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/East_River" title="East River">East River</a> Esplanade – Manhattan</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/NY_Waterway" title="NY Waterway">NY Waterway Ferry</a> – Manhattan to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jersey_City,_NJ" title="Jersey City, NJ">Jersey City, NJ</a></li></ul>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:199px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:LWGT_ECGW_sign_JC_Belmont_%26_Summit_Av_jeh.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2555" data-file-width="1534" height="329" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/LWGT_ECGW_sign_JC_Belmont_%26_Summit_Av_jeh.jpg/197px-LWGT_ECGW_sign_JC_Belmont_%26_Summit_Av_jeh.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/LWGT_ECGW_sign_JC_Belmont_%26_Summit_Av_jeh.jpg/296px-LWGT_ECGW_sign_JC_Belmont_%26_Summit_Av_jeh.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/LWGT_ECGW_sign_JC_Belmont_%26_Summit_Av_jeh.jpg/395px-LWGT_ECGW_sign_JC_Belmont_%26_Summit_Av_jeh.jpg 2x" width="197"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:LWGT_ECGW_sign_JC_Belmont_%26_Summit_Av_jeh.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Near <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Park_(Jersey_City)" title="Lincoln Park (Jersey City)">Lincoln Park (Jersey City)</a></div></div></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Jersey">New Jersey</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: New Jersey">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The New Jersey section of the greenway is accessed from New York across the <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">Hudson River</a> by the <a href="/wiki/George_Washington_Bridge" title="George Washington Bridge">George Washington Bridge</a> or ferry, and from <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">Pennsylvania</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Calhoun_Street_Bridge" title="Calhoun Street Bridge">Calhoun Street Bridge</a> across the <a href="/wiki/Delaware_River" title="Delaware River">Delaware River</a>. The route travels through <a href="/wiki/Jersey_City,_New_Jersey" title="Jersey City, New Jersey">Jersey City</a>, <a href="/wiki/Newark,_New_Jersey" title="Newark, New Jersey">Newark</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Brunswick,_New_Jersey" title="New Brunswick, New Jersey">New Brunswick</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Trenton,_New_Jersey" title="Trenton, New Jersey">Trenton</a> while also traveling through rural areas. New Jersey has the second-highest percentage of off-road trails at 54%.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Hudson_River_Waterfront_Walkway" title="Hudson River Waterfront Walkway">Hudson River Waterfront Walkway</a> – <a href="/wiki/Jersey_City,_New_Jersey" title="Jersey City, New Jersey">Jersey City</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Park_(Jersey_City)" title="Lincoln Park (Jersey City)">Lincoln Park Path</a> – Jersey City</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wittpenn_Bridge" title="Wittpenn Bridge">Wittpenn Bridge</a> (once completed circa 2022)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
<li>Newark Riverfront Trail – <a href="/wiki/Newark,_New_Jersey" title="Newark, New Jersey">Newark</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rahway_River_Parkway" title="Rahway River Parkway">Rahway River Parkway</a> – <a href="/wiki/Union_County,_New_Jersey" title="Union County, New Jersey">Union County</a>
<ul><li>Black Brook Park Path – <a href="/wiki/Kenilworth,_New_Jersey" title="Kenilworth, New Jersey">Kenilworth</a></li>
<li>Lenape Park Path – <a href="/wiki/Union_County,_New_Jersey" title="Union County, New Jersey">Union County</a></li>
<li>Nomahegan Park Path – <a href="/wiki/Cranford,_New_Jersey" title="Cranford, New Jersey">Cranford</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Roosevelt_Park_(Edison,_New_Jersey)" title="Roosevelt Park (Edison, New Jersey)">Roosevelt Park</a> Path – <a href="/wiki/Edison,_New_Jersey" title="Edison, New Jersey">Edison</a></li>
<li>Merrill Park Path – <a href="/wiki/Middlesex_County,_New_Jersey" title="Middlesex County, New Jersey">Middlesex County</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Middlesex_Greenway_(New_Jersey)" title="Middlesex Greenway (New Jersey)">Middlesex Greenway</a> – Middlesex County</li>
<li>Donaldson Park Path – Middlesex County</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Johnson_Park_(New_Jersey)" title="Johnson Park (New Jersey)">Johnson Park</a> Path – <a href="/wiki/Piscataway,_New_Jersey" title="Piscataway, New Jersey">Piscataway</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Landing_Lane_Bridge" title="Landing Lane Bridge">Landing Lane Bridge</a> Path – Piscataway &amp; <a href="/wiki/New_Brunswick,_New_Jersey" title="New Brunswick, New Jersey">New Brunswick</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/D%26R_Canal_Trail" title="D&amp;R Canal Trail">D&amp;R Canal Trail</a> – New Brunswick &amp; <a href="/wiki/Trenton,_New_Jersey" title="Trenton, New Jersey">Trenton</a></li>
<li>D&amp;R Canal Towpath – <a href="/wiki/Hamilton_Township,_Mercer_County,_New_Jersey" title="Hamilton Township, Mercer County, New Jersey">Hamilton</a> &amp; <a href="/wiki/Bordentown,_New_Jersey" title="Bordentown, New Jersey">Bordentown</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Calhoun_Street_Bridge" title="Calhoun Street Bridge">Calhoun Street Bridge</a> – <a href="/wiki/Trenton,_New_Jersey" title="Trenton, New Jersey">Trenton, New Jersey</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Morrisville,_Bucks_County,_Pennsylvania" title="Morrisville, Bucks County, Pennsylvania">Morrisville, Pennsylvania</a></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pennsylvania">Pennsylvania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Pennsylvania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:308px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Schuykill-river-trail-philadelphia-pa.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="750" data-file-width="1000" height="230" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Schuykill-river-trail-philadelphia-pa.jpg/306px-Schuykill-river-trail-philadelphia-pa.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Schuykill-river-trail-philadelphia-pa.jpg/459px-Schuykill-river-trail-philadelphia-pa.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Schuykill-river-trail-philadelphia-pa.jpg/612px-Schuykill-river-trail-philadelphia-pa.jpg 2x" width="306"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Schuykill-river-trail-philadelphia-pa.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Schuykill River Trail in Philadelphia</div></div></div>
<p>The greenway travels through the smaller towns of <a href="/wiki/Bucks_County,_Pennsylvania" title="Bucks County, Pennsylvania">Bucks County,</a> then through the city of <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">Philadelphia</a>, where it passes numerous historical landmarks and travels over <a href="/wiki/Spring_Garden_Street_Bridge" title="Spring Garden Street Bridge">Spring Garden Street</a>, the city's most bicycle-friendly street. The route follows the <a href="/wiki/Schuylkill_River_Trail" title="Schuylkill River Trail">Schuylkill River Trail</a> south towards Delaware. The 67-mile (108 km) route is 31% off-road, but there is a third of the trail that has no route yet. Planning is being done to close the gaps.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Delaware_Canal_State_Park" title="Delaware Canal State Park">Delaware Canal State Park</a> Trail – <a href="/wiki/Bucks_County,_Pennsylvania" title="Bucks County, Pennsylvania">Bucks County</a></li>
<li>Bristol Spur Line Park Trail – <a href="/wiki/Bristol,_Pennsylvania" title="Bristol, Pennsylvania">Bristol</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pennypack_Creek" title="Pennypack Creek">Pennypack Creek</a> Park Trail – <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">Philadelphia</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Port_Richmond,_Philadelphia" title="Port Richmond, Philadelphia">Port Richmond</a> Trail – Philadelphia</li>
<li>K&amp;T Trail at Lardner's Point Park – Philadelphia</li>
<li>Penn Street Trail – Philadelphia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Schuylkill_River_Trail" title="Schuylkill River Trail">Schuylkill River Trail</a> – Philadelphia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bartram%27s_Garden" title="Bartram's Garden">Bartram's Gardens</a> Trail – Philadelphia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Grays_Ferry,_Philadelphia" title="Grays Ferry, Philadelphia">Grays Ferry Crescent</a> – Philadelphia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cobbs_Creek" title="Cobbs Creek">Cobbs Creek</a> Trail – Philadelphia</li>
<li>58th Street Connector – Philadelphia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_Heinz_National_Wildlife_Refuge_at_Tinicum" title="John Heinz National Wildlife Refuge at Tinicum">Heinz NWR</a> Trail – Philadelphia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania_Route_291" title="Pennsylvania Route 291">Route 291</a> Sidepath – <a href="/wiki/Eddystone,_Pennsylvania" title="Eddystone, Pennsylvania">Eddystone</a></li>
<li>Chester Riverwalk – <a href="/wiki/Chester,_Pennsylvania" title="Chester, Pennsylvania">Chester</a></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Delaware">Delaware</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Delaware">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:274px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Northern-delaware-greenway-wilmington-de.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="750" data-file-width="1000" height="204" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Northern-delaware-greenway-wilmington-de.jpg/272px-Northern-delaware-greenway-wilmington-de.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Northern-delaware-greenway-wilmington-de.jpg/408px-Northern-delaware-greenway-wilmington-de.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Northern-delaware-greenway-wilmington-de.jpg/544px-Northern-delaware-greenway-wilmington-de.jpg 2x" width="272"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Northern-delaware-greenway-wilmington-de.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Northern Delaware Greenway in <a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_Delaware" title="Wilmington, Delaware">Wilmington</a></div></div></div>
<p>The greenway runs for 43 miles (69 km) through Delaware. Greenway users travel down the Northern Delaware Greenway to historic <a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_Delaware" title="Wilmington, Delaware">Wilmington</a> and continue on to the <a href="/wiki/Christina_River" title="Christina River">Christina Riverwalk</a>. Next, travelers head to historic <a href="/wiki/New_Castle,_Delaware" title="New Castle, Delaware">New Castle</a> and ride along the New Castle Riverfront before reaching <a href="/wiki/Newark,_Delaware" title="Newark, Delaware">Newark</a> and heading west towards Maryland.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Northern Delaware Greenway – <a href="/wiki/New_Castle_County,_Delaware" title="New Castle County, Delaware">New Castle County</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Christina_River" title="Christina River">Christina Riverwalk</a> – <a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_Delaware" title="Wilmington, Delaware">Wilmington</a></li>
<li>Jack A. Markell Trail – <a href="/wiki/New_Castle,_Delaware" title="New Castle, Delaware">New Castle</a></li>
<li>New Castle Riverfront Greenway – New Castle</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Penn_Farm_of_the_Trustees_of_the_New_Castle_Common" title="Penn Farm of the Trustees of the New Castle Common">Penn Farm Trail</a> – New Castle</li>
<li>Churchmans Rd. Sidepath – New Castle County</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Delaware_Route_4" title="Delaware Route 4">Delaware Route 4</a> sidepath – New Castle County</li>
<li>Library Rd. Sidepath – <a href="/wiki/Newark,_Delaware" title="Newark, Delaware">Newark</a></li>
<li>James F. Hall Trail – Newark</li></ul>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:NCR_mile_marker_ECG.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3264" data-file-width="1952" height="334" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/NCR_mile_marker_ECG.jpg/200px-NCR_mile_marker_ECG.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/NCR_mile_marker_ECG.jpg/300px-NCR_mile_marker_ECG.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/NCR_mile_marker_ECG.jpg/400px-NCR_mile_marker_ECG.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:NCR_mile_marker_ECG.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>One of the mile markers on the <a href="/wiki/Torrey_C._Brown_Rail_Trail" title="Torrey C. Brown Rail Trail">Torrey C. Brown Rail Trail</a>, showing its designation as part of the East Coast Greenway.</div></div></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Maryland">Maryland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Maryland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The route starts in <a href="/wiki/Elkton,_Maryland" title="Elkton, Maryland">Elkton, Maryland</a>, and heads west to <a href="/wiki/Perryville,_Maryland" title="Perryville, Maryland">Perryville</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Susquehanna_River" title="Susquehanna River">Susquehanna River</a>. Travelers pass the <a href="/wiki/Perry_Point,_Maryland" title="Perry Point, Maryland">Perry Point</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/VA_Medical_Center" title="VA Medical Center">VA Medical Center</a> and have great views of the <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">Chesapeake Bay</a>. Users cross the Susquehanna at the <a href="/wiki/Thomas_J._Hatem_Memorial_Bridge" title="Thomas J. Hatem Memorial Bridge">Thomas J. Hatem Memorial Bridge</a>, but they are limited to crossing between dawn and dusk on weekends, holidays, and special events that have been arranged in advance, and they must be at least 18 years old or have a valid driver's license.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Havre_de_Grace,_Maryland" title="Havre de Grace, Maryland">Havre de Grace</a> is after the bridge, followed by <a href="/wiki/Harford_County,_Maryland" title="Harford County, Maryland">Harford County</a>, <a href="/wiki/Monkton,_Maryland" title="Monkton, Maryland">Monkton</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Cockeysville,_Maryland" title="Cockeysville, Maryland">Cockeysville</a>. Next, riders travel south through <a href="/wiki/Baltimore" title="Baltimore">Baltimore</a> and then on to <a href="/wiki/Annapolis,_Maryland" title="Annapolis, Maryland">Annapolis</a> before finishing the 166-mile (267 km) stretch of greenway in <a href="/wiki/Hyattsville,_Maryland" title="Hyattsville, Maryland">Hyattsville</a> and entering <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> 32% of the route is off-road.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Torrey_C._Brown_Rail_Trail" title="Torrey C. Brown Rail Trail">Torrey C. Brown Rail Trail</a> – MD border to Ashland (<a href="/wiki/Cockeysville,_Maryland" title="Cockeysville, Maryland">Cockeysville</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jones_Falls_Trail" title="Jones Falls Trail">Jones Falls Trail</a> – Baltimore</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gwynns_Falls_Trail" title="Gwynns Falls Trail">Gwynns Falls Trail</a> – Baltimore</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BWI_Trail" title="BWI Trail">BWI Trail</a> – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BWI_Airport" title="BWI Airport">BWI Airport</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Baltimore_%26_Annapolis_Trail" title="Baltimore &amp; Annapolis Trail">Baltimore &amp; Annapolis Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Glen_Burnie,_Maryland" title="Glen Burnie, Maryland">Glen Burnie</a> to Annapolis</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cross_Island_Trail" title="Cross Island Trail">Cross Island Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Queen_Anne%27s_County,_Maryland" title="Queen Anne's County, Maryland">Queen Anne's County</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Colonial_Annapolis_Historic_District" title="Colonial Annapolis Historic District">Colonial Annapolis Maritime Trail System</a> – Annapolis</li>
<li>South Shore Trail – <a href="/wiki/Anne_Arundel_County,_Maryland" title="Anne Arundel County, Maryland">Anne Arundel County</a></li>
<li>Odenton Road Bicycle Path – <a href="/wiki/Odenton,_Maryland" title="Odenton, Maryland">Odenton</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Washington,_Baltimore_and_Annapolis_Trail" title="Washington, Baltimore and Annapolis Trail">Washington, Baltimore and Annapolis Trail</a> – Anne Arundel County</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Anacostia_Tributary_Trail_System" title="Anacostia Tributary Trail System">Anacostia Tributary Trail System</a> – <a href="/wiki/Prince_George%27s_County,_Maryland" title="Prince George's County, Maryland">Prince George's County</a></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="District_of_Columbia">District of Columbia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: District of Columbia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Scott-Bauer_USDA--e1458072528659.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="388" data-file-width="250" height="341" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Scott-Bauer_USDA--e1458072528659.jpg/220px-Scott-Bauer_USDA--e1458072528659.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/9/92/Scott-Bauer_USDA--e1458072528659.jpg 1.5x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Scott-Bauer_USDA--e1458072528659.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>View of the <a href="/wiki/Washington_Monument" title="Washington Monument">Washington Monument</a> and <a href="/wiki/National_Cherry_Blossom_Festival" title="National Cherry Blossom Festival">cherry blossoms</a> from the East Coast Greenway</div></div></div>
<p>From the Maryland state line, the Greenway follows the <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Branch_Trail" title="Metropolitan Branch Trail">Metropolitan Branch Trail</a> to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Union_Station_(Washington,_D.C.)" title="Union Station (Washington, D.C.)">Union Station</a> and then the <a href="/wiki/National_Mall" title="National Mall">National Mall</a>, the ECG's official midpoint. Greenway users can then travel on towards the <a href="/wiki/Arlington_Memorial_Bridge" title="Arlington Memorial Bridge">Arlington Memorial Bridge</a> over the <a href="/wiki/Potomac_River" title="Potomac River">Potomac River</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Mount_Vernon_Trail" title="Mount Vernon Trail">Mount Vernon Trail</a> into Virginia. Just under half of the 8-mile (13 km) segment through the District is off-road; the downtown area offers no off-road option.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dc_15-0"><a href="#cite_note-dc-15">[15]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Branch_Trail" title="Metropolitan Branch Trail">Metropolitan Branch Trail</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/National_Mall" title="National Mall">National Mall Path</a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="South_Atlantic_region">South Atlantic region</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: South Atlantic region">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Virginia">Virginia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Virginia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>This segment travels from Washington, D.C., to <a href="/wiki/Mount_Vernon" title="Mount Vernon">Mount Vernon</a>, heads towards <a href="/wiki/Fredericksburg,_Virginia" title="Fredericksburg, Virginia">Fredericksburg</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Potomac_Heritage_Trail" title="Potomac Heritage Trail">Potomac Heritage Trail</a>, and continues on to the state capital of <a href="/wiki/Richmond,_Virginia" title="Richmond, Virginia">Richmond</a>. At this point, the greenway splits: the 300-mile (480 km) spine route (16% off-road) continues southwest to the <a href="/wiki/Piedmont_(United_States)" title="Piedmont (United States)">Piedmont</a> region of North Carolina. The alternate route, the 140-mile (230 km) Historic Coastal Route (46% off-road), travels southeast through <a href="/wiki/Jamestown,_Virginia" title="Jamestown, Virginia">Jamestown</a> and <a href="/wiki/Williamsburg,_Virginia" title="Williamsburg, Virginia">Williamsburg</a>, then towards <a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_North_Carolina" title="Wilmington, North Carolina">Wilmington, North Carolina</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Mount_Vernon_Trail" title="Mount Vernon Trail">Mount Vernon Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Arlington_Memorial_Bridge" title="Arlington Memorial Bridge">Arlington Memorial Bridge</a>, Washington, D.C., to <a href="/wiki/Mount_Vernon" title="Mount Vernon">Mount Vernon</a></li>
<li>Silverbrook Road Multi-use Trail – <a href="/wiki/Fairfax_County,_Virginia" title="Fairfax County, Virginia">Fairfax County</a></li>
<li>Ox Road Multi-use Trail – Fairfax County</li>
<li>Richmond Highway Multi-use Trail – Fairfax County</li>
<li>Telegraph Road Multi-use Trail – Fairfax County</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fairfax_County_Parkway" title="Fairfax County Parkway">Fairfax County Parkway</a> Multi-use Trail – Fairfax County</li>
<li>Grist Mill Park Multi-use Trail – Fairfax County</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Virginia_Central_Railway" title="Virginia Central Railway">Virginia Central Railway Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Fredericksburg,_Virginia" title="Fredericksburg, Virginia">Fredericksburg</a></li>
<li>Ashland Railside Park Trail – <a href="/wiki/Ashland,_Virginia" title="Ashland, Virginia">Ashland</a></li>
<li>Cannon Creek Greenway – Cannon Creek Greenway</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Belle_Isle_(Richmond,_Virginia)" title="Belle Isle (Richmond, Virginia)">Belle Isle</a> Bridge – <a href="/wiki/Richmond,_Virginia" title="Richmond, Virginia">Richmond</a></li>
<li>Belle Isle Trail – Richmond</li>
<li>Lower <a href="/wiki/Appomattox_River" title="Appomattox River">Appomattox River</a> Trail – <a href="/wiki/Petersburg,_Virginia" title="Petersburg, Virginia">Petersburg</a></li>
<li>Tobacco Heritage Trail – <a href="/wiki/Lawrenceville,_Virginia" title="Lawrenceville, Virginia">Lawrenceville</a>, <a href="/wiki/La_Crosse,_Virginia" title="La Crosse, Virginia">La Crosse</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Brodnax,_Virginia" title="Brodnax, Virginia">Brodnax</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Virginia_Capital_Trail" title="Virginia Capital Trail">Virginia Capital Trail</a> – Richmond to <a href="/wiki/Williamsburg,_Virginia" title="Williamsburg, Virginia">Williamsburg</a></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="North_Carolina">North Carolina</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Coast_Greenway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: North Carolina">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4><p>
The Greenway's spine route travels south through rural <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">North Carolina</a> into the <a href="/wiki/Research_Triangle" title="Research Triangle">Research Triangle Region</a>, passing through <a href="/wiki/Durham,_North_Carolina" title="Durham, North Carolina">Durham</a>, <a href="/wiki/Raleigh,_North_Carolina" title="Raleigh, North Carolina">Raleigh</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Cary,_North_Carolina" title="Cary, North Carolina">Cary</a>. This section is on the <a href="/wiki/American_Tobacco_Trail" title="American Tobacco Trail">American Tobacco Trail</a>, which runs past the East Coast Greenway Alliance Headquarters in Durham. The route continues southwest through the <a href="/wiki/Sandhills_(Carolina)" title="Sandhills (Carolina)">Sandhills</a> region and into <a href="/wiki/Fayetteville,_North_Carolina" title="Fayetteville, North Carolina">Fayetteville</a> before following the <a href="/wiki/Cape_Fear_River" title="Cape Fear River">Cape Fear River</a> into <a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_North_Carolina" title="Wilmington, North Carolina">Wilmington</a> and traveling along the coast. Alternatively, the Historic Coast Route, entering from southeastern Virginia, moves onto the <a href="/wiki/Dismal_Swamp_Canal" title="Dismal Swamp Canal">Dismal Swamp Canal Trail</a> and follows the coast down through <a href="/wiki/Greenville,_North_Carolina" title="Greenville, North Carolina">Greenville</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jacksonville,_North_Carolina" title="Jacksonville, North Carolina">Jacksonville</a> before reaching Wilmington where the routes connect. The 372-mile (599 km) spine route is 25% off-road at this time.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup></p><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:377px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Raleigh-NC_Little-Rock-trail-570x430.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="430" data-file-width="570" height="283" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Raleigh-NC_Little-Rock-trail-570x430.jpg/375px-Raleigh-NC_Little-Rock-trail-570x430.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Raleigh-NC_Little-Rock-trail-570x430.jpg/563px-Raleigh-NC_Little-Rock-trail-570x430.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/d0/Raleigh-NC_Little-Rock-trail-570x430.jpg 2x" width="375"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Raleigh-NC_Little-Rock-trail-570x430.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Little Rock Trail in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Raleigh,_NC" title="Raleigh, NC">Raleigh, NC</a></div></div></div>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ellerbe_Creek_Trail" title="Ellerbe Creek Trail">Ellerbe Creek Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Durham,_North_Carolina" title="Durham, North Carolina">Durham</a></li>
<li>South Ellerbee Creek Trail – Durham</li>
<li>Downtown Trail – Durham</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/American_Tobacco_Trail" title="American Tobacco Trail">American Tobacco Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/Durham_County,_North_Carolina" title="Durham County, North Carolina">Durham County</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chatham_County,_North_Carolina" title="Chatham County, North Carolina">Chatham County</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Wake_County,_North_Carolina" title="Wake County, North Carolina">Wake County</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Black_Creek,_North_Carolina" title="Black Creek, North Carolina">Black Creek</a> Greenway – <a href="/wiki/Cary,_North_Carolina" title="Cary, North Carolina">Cary</a></li>
<li>White Oak Greenway – Cary</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Umstead_State_Park" title="Umstead State Park">Umstead State Park</a> Trail – Wake County</li>
<li>Reedy Creek Greenway – <a href="/wiki/Raleigh,_North_Carolina" title="Raleigh, North Carolina">Raleigh</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Walnut_Creek,_North_Carolina" title="Walnut Creek, North Carolina">Walnut Creek</a> Trail – Raleigh</li>
<li>Rocky Branch Trail – Raleigh</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pullen_Park" title="Pullen Park">Pullen Park Trail</a> – Raleigh</li>
<li>Little Rock Trail – Raleigh</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Walnut_Creek,_North_Carolina" title="Walnut Creek, North Carolina">Lower Walnut Creek Trail</a> – Raleigh</li>
<li>Chavis Way Sidepath – Raleigh</li>
<li>Central Raleigh Trail – Raleigh</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Neuse_River_Trail" title="Neuse River Trail">Neuse River Trail</a> – Raleigh &amp; <a href="/wiki/Clayton,_North_Carolina" title="Clayton, North Carolina">Clayton</a></li>
<li>Buffalo Creek Greenway – <a href="/wiki/Smithfield,_North_Carolina" title="Smithfield, North Carolina">Smithfield</a></li>
<li>Dunn-Erwin Trail – <a href="/wiki/Dunn,_North_Carolina" title="Dunn, North Carolina">Dunn</a> &amp; <a href="/wiki/Erwin,_North_Carolina" title="Erwin, North Carolina">Erwin</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cape_Fear_River" title="Cape Fear River">Cape Fear River</a> Trail – <a href="/wiki/Fayetteville,_North_Carolina" title="Fayetteville, North Carolina">Fayetteville</a></li>
<li>Jacksonville Rail-Trail – <a href="/wiki/Jacksonville,_North_Carolina" title="Jacksonville, North Carolina">Jacksonville</a></li>
<li>Greenfield Lake Path – <a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_North_Carolina" title="Wilmington, North Carolina">Wilmington</a></li>
<li>Wilmington Riverwalk – Wilmington</li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Dismal_Swamp_Canal" title="Dismal Swamp Canal">Dismal Swamp Canal Trail</a> – <a href="/wiki/South_Mills,_North_Carolina" title="South Mills, North Carolina">South Mills</a></li>
<li>Carolina Beach Greenway – <a href="/wiki/Carolina_Beach,_North_Carolina" title="Carolina Beach, North Carolina">Carolina Beach</a></li>
